# Layers

Copy page

This example shows how to use the extends key in \`nuxt.config.ts\`.

This example shows how to use the `extends` key in `nuxt.config.ts` to use the `base/` directory as a base Nuxt application, and use its components, composables or config and override them if necessary.

[](../../../../../external.html?link=https://nuxt.com/docs/getting-started/layers)Read more in Docs > Getting Started > Layers.

    -   [Testing](testing)
    -   [useCookie](use-cookie)
    -   [Use Custom Fetch Composable](use-custom-fetch-composable)
    
-   Experimental
    
    -   [WASM](../experimental/wasm)

# Locale

Copy page

This example shows how to define a locale composable to handle the application's locale, both server and client side.

You can right-click to "View Page Source" and see that Nuxt renders the correct date in SSR based on the visitor's locale.

# Teleport

Copy page

This example shows how to use the <Teleport> with client-side and server-side rendering.

Vue 3 provides the [`<Teleport>` component](../../../../../external.html?link=https://vuejs.org/guide/built-ins/teleport.html) which allows content to be rendered elsewhere in the DOM, outside of the Vue application.

This example shows how to use the `<Teleport>` with client-side and server-side rendering.

[](../../../../../external.html?link=https://nuxt.com/docs/api/components/teleports)Read more in Docs > API > Components > Teleports.

# useCookie

Copy page

This example shows how to use the useCookie API to persist small amounts of data that both client and server can use.

[](../../../../../external.html?link=https://nuxt.com/docs/api/composables/use-cookie)Read more in Docs > API > Composables > Use Cookie.

# Use Custom Fetch Composable

Copy page

This example shows a convenient wrapper for the useFetch composable from nuxt. It allows you to customize the fetch request with default values and user authentication token.

[](../../../../../external.html?link=https://nuxt.com/docs/guide/recipes/custom-usefetch)Read more in Docs > Guide > Recipes > Custom Usefetch.

# Auto Imports

Copy page

This example demonstrates the auto-imports feature in Nuxt.

Example of the auto-imports feature in Nuxt with:

-   Vue components in the `components/` directory are auto-imported and can be used directly in your templates.
-   Vue composables in the `composables/` directory are auto-imported and can be used directly in your templates and JS/TS files.
-   JS/TS variables and functions in the `utils/` directory are auto-imported and can be used directly in your templates and JS/TS files.

[](../../../../../external.html?link=https://nuxt.com/docs/guide/directory-structure/components)Read more in Docs > Guide > Directory Structure > Components.

[](../../../../../external.html?link=https://nuxt.com/docs/guide/directory-structure/composables)Read more in Docs > Guide > Directory Structure > Composables.

[](../../../../../external.html?link=https://nuxt.com/docs/guide/directory-structure/utils)Read more in Docs > Guide > Directory Structure > Utils.

# Data Fetching

Copy page

This example demonstrates data fetching with Nuxt using built-in composables and API routes.

# State Management

Copy page

This example shows how to use the \`useState\` composable to create a reactive and SSR-friendly shared state across components.

[](../../../../../external.html?link=https://nuxt.com/docs/getting-started/state-management)Read more in Docs > Getting Started > State Management.

[](../../../../../external.html?link=https://nuxt.com/docs/api/composables/use-state)Read more in Docs > API > Composables > Use State.

    -   [Teleport](../advanced/teleport)

    -   [Use Custom Fetch Composable](../advanced/use-custom-fetch-composable)
    
-   Experimental
    
    -   [WASM](../experimental/wasm)

# Middleware

Copy page

This example shows how to add route middleware with the middleware/ directory or with a plugin, and how to use them globally or per page.

[](../../../../../external.html?link=https://nuxt.com/docs/guide/directory-structure/middleware)Read more in Docs > Guide > Directory Structure > Middleware.

# Universal Router

This example demonstrates Nuxt universal routing utilities without depending on \`pages/\` and \`vue-router\`.
